   - **Sub-task 5:** Combine all costs to produce a total budget and summary breakdown.

4) **Data Planning**
   - From the **environment**:
     - Retrieve the user’s name for correspondence and document initiation.
     - Check if the user has any prior mortgage or banking relationship that might affect financing.
     - Review calendar or schedule for possible move-in timelines.

     - Request property listings in Toronto that meet the 2–3 bedroom, CAD $700K–$850K criteria.
     - Gather details on property type, location, price, and condition.

5) **Anticipated Changes**
   - The user’s preferences (e.g., location within Toronto, condo vs. detached home) may evolve once listings are reviewed.
   - Financing options may need adjustment depending on creditworthiness and lender offerings.
   - Moving and setup service costs may vary depending on property location and timing.
